Conclusion: 研究发现纯文本输入下模型的空间推理能力存在显著缺陷，通过分析发现了模型绑合视点与观测的机制问题，提出的选择性微调方法为提升模型空间智能提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Over the past year, spatial intelligence has drawn increasing attention. Many prior works study it from the perspective of visual-spatial intelligence, where models have access to visuospatial information from visual inputs. However, in the absence of visual information, whether linguistic intelligence alone is sufficient to endow models with spatial intelligence, and how models perform relevant tasks with text-only inputs still remain unexplored. Therefore, in this paper, we focus on a fundamental and critical capability in spatial intelligence from a linguistic perspective: viewpoint rotation understanding (VRU). Specifically, LLMs and VLMs are asked to infer their final viewpoint and predict the corresponding observation in an environment given textual description of viewpoint rotation and observation over multiple steps. We find that both LLMs and VLMs perform poorly on our proposed dataset while human can easily achieve 100% accuracy, indicating a substantial gap between current model capabilities and the requirements of spatial intelligence. To uncover the underlying mechanisms, we conduct a layer-wise probing analysis and head-wise causal intervention. Our findings reveal that although models encode viewpoint information in the hidden states, they appear to struggle to bind the viewpoint position with corresponding observation, resulting in a hallucination in final layers. Finally, we selectively fine-tune the key attention heads identified by causal intervention to improve VRU performance. Experimental results demonstrate that such selective fine-tuning achieves improved VRU performance while avoiding catastrophic forgetting of generic abilities. Our dataset and code will be released at https://github.com/Young-Zhen/VRU_Interpret .

</details>


### [204] [Diagnosing LLM Judge Reliability: Conformal Prediction Sets and Transitivity Violations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15302)
*Manan Gupta,Dhruv Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过两方面的诊断工具包分析LLM作为裁判在文本生成评价中的可靠性，发现聚合指标下隐藏的普遍不一致性，并为每个实例提供了理论可靠的置信区间作为可靠性指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然基于大语言模型的自动评价框架在自然语言生成评估中应用日益广泛，但其单例可靠性尚不清楚，需要更深入的分析工具来理解评价的不确定性。

Method: 在SummEval数据集上应用了两方面诊断：(1)传递性分析揭示掩藏在低聚合违规率下的普遍单输入不一致性；(2)使用分离一致性预测方法生成带有理论保证的得分区间，区间宽度作为单例可靠性指标。

Result: 研究发现33%-67%的文档至少存在一个有向3环，传递性违规严重；预测区间宽度在评价者间具有一致性，表明其捕捉的是文档难度而非评价者噪声；相关性评价最可靠，流畅性和一致性最不可靠。

Conclusion: LLM作为裁判的可靠性在不同评价标准间差异显著，使用预测区间宽度可以作为单例可靠性的有效指标，评价标准比具体评价者更重要，相关性和连贯性评价相对可靠，而流畅性和一致性评价需要更多改进。

Abstract: LLM-as-judge frameworks are increasingly used for automatic NLG evaluation, yet their per-instance reliability remains poorly understood. We present a two-pronged diagnostic toolkit applied to SummEval: $\textbf{(1)}$ a transitivity analysis that reveals widespread per-input inconsistency masked by low aggregate violation rates ($\barρ = 0.8$-$4.1\%$), with $33$-$67\%$ of documents exhibiting at least one directed 3-cycle; and $\textbf{(2)}$ split conformal prediction sets over 1-5 Likert scores providing theoretically-guaranteed $\geq(1{-}α)$ coverage, with set width serving as a per-instance reliability indicator ($r_s = {+}0.576$, $N{=}1{,}918$, $p < 10^{-100}$, pooled across all judges). Critically, prediction set width shows consistent cross-judge agreement ($\bar{r} = 0.32$-$0.38$), demonstrating it captures document-level difficulty rather than judge-specific noise. Across four judges and four criteria, both diagnostics converge: criterion matters more than judge, with relevance judged most reliably (avg. set size $\approx 3.0$) and coherence moderately so (avg. set size $\approx 3.9$), while fluency and consistency remain unreliable (avg. set size $\approx 4.9$). We release all code, prompts, and cached results.

</details>


### [205] [Generalization in LLM Problem Solving: The Case of the Shortest Path](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15306)
*Yao Tong,Jiayuan Ye,Anastasia Borovykh,Reza Shokri*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究通过一个受控的寻路规划环境评估语言模型的系统性泛化能力，发现模型在空间迁移上有良好表现，但在长度扩展方面存在递归不稳定性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究难以分离训练数据、训练范式和推理策略等因素对语言模型系统性泛化能力的影响，需要一个可控环境来准确定位失败原因。

Method: 建立一个基于最短路径规划的受控合成环境，支持空间迁移和长度扩展两个正交的泛化维度，分析不同学习阶段对系统性问题解决能力的影响。

Result: 模型在空间迁移上表现良好，但在长度扩展上始终失败，原因是递归不稳定性；数据覆盖范围限定了能力边界，强化学习改善训练稳定性但不扩展边界，推理时间扩展提升性能但无法解决长度扩展失败。

Conclusion: 语言模型在系统性泛化能力上存在明显局限，特别是在处理长序列时的递归不稳定性问题，需要新的方法来突破数据覆盖和长度扩展限制。

Abstract: Whether language models can systematically generalize remains actively debated. Yet empirical performance is jointly shaped by multiple factors such as training data, training paradigms, and inference-time strategies, making failures difficult to interpret. We introduce a controlled synthetic environment based on shortest-path planning, a canonical composable sequential optimization problem. The setup enables clean separation of these factors and supports two orthogonal axes of generalization: spatial transfer to unseen maps and length scaling to longer-horizon problems. We find that models exhibit strong spatial transfer but consistently fail under length scaling due to recursive instability. We further analyze how distinct stages of the learning pipeline influence systematic problem-solving: for example, data coverage sets capability limits; reinforcement learning improves training stability but does not expand those limits; and inference-time scaling enhances performance but cannot rescue length-scaling failures.

</details>

### [206] [A Synonymous Variational Perspective on the Rate-Distortion-Perception Tradeoff](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14603)
*Zijian Liang,Kai Niu,Changshuo Wang,Jin Xu,Ping Zhang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 基于语义信息理论，从同义集重建角度重新解释感知压缩，建立同义变分推理框架，证明同义率失真感知理论的一致性，阐明了分布差异项的起源和与传统RDP理论及经典RD理论的兼容性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典率失真理论通过编码率和重建失真的权衡描述信号压缩极限，然而现有的率失真感知框架引入的感知质量度量（基于分布的散度）作为一个建模原则而非理论推导结果，其理论起源尚不明确。本文从一个基于同义性的语义信息视角出发，旨在从理论上厘清感知压缩的本质。

Method: 1. 将感知重建重新表述为在理想同义集内恢复任一可接受样本而非源样本本身，相应地建立了同义信源编码架构。
2. 提出了同义变分推理分析框架，引入了同义变分下界来实现对同义集导向压缩的可处理分析。
3. 在此框架内建立了同义性-感知一致性原则，并从推导结果出发证明了同义率失真感知权衡关系。

Result: 1. 证明了语义信息的最优识别在理论上与感知优化是一致的（同义性-感知一致性原则）。
2. 证明了所提出的同义信源编码存在一个同义率失真感知权衡。
3. 分析结果表明：从基于同义集的重建目标出发，分布差异项自然地产生，阐明了其与现有RDP公式以及经典RD理论的兼容性，并暗示了同义信源编码的潜在优势。

Conclusion: 本文从一个基于同义集的语义信息视角为感知压缩提供了新的理论解释框架。它揭示了感知质量度量的理论起源（源自同义集重建目标），建立了其与传统率失真理论和现有RDP理论的联系，并指出了同义信源编码潜在的优越性。这项工作为理解信号压缩中的感知问题提供了更深层的理论基础。

Abstract: The fundamental limit of natural signal compression has traditionally been characterized by classical rate-distortion (RD) theory through the tradeoff between coding rate and reconstruction distortion, while the rate-distortion-perception (RDP) framework introduces a divergence-based measure of perceptual quality as a modeling principle rather than a theoretically-derived principle, leaving its theoretical origin unclear. In this paper, motivated by a synonymity-based semantic information perspective, we reformulate perceptual reconstruction as recovering any admissible sample within an ideal synonymous set (synset) associated with the source, rather than the source sample itself, and correspondingly establish a synonymous source coding architecture. On this basis, we develop a synonymous variational inference (SVI) analysis framework with a synonymous variational lower bound (SVLBO) for tractable analysis of synset-oriented compression. Within this framework, we establish a synonymity-perception consistency principle, showing that optimal identification of semantic information is theoretically consistent with perceptual optimization. Based on its derivation result, we prove a synonymous RDP tradeoff for the proposed synonymous source coding. These analytical results show that the distributional divergence term arises naturally from the synset-based reconstruction objective, clarify its compatibility with existing RDP formulations and classical RD theory, and suggest the potential advantages of synonymous source coding.

### [207] [Sidorenko-Inspired Pessimistic Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14647)
*Yu-Ting Lin,Hsin-Po Wang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的基于毛毛虫图的信息论框架，用于多表连接大小的上限估计，相比之前的星形图和双星形图方法有显著改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前Abo Khamis等人使用星形图的图同态计数来估计连接大小，后续工作扩展到双星形图。本文进一步扩展到毛毛虫图这一更大图类，以提供更精确的连接大小上限估计。

Method: 1. 将连接大小上限问题转化为信息熵上界问题
2. 使用香农型不等式将联合熵分解为局部熵
3. 利用毛毛虫图到表的图同态统计来估计局部熵上界
4. 所有同态计数可在连接表大小的线性时间内完成

Result: 1. 星形图方法高估连接大小约m倍
2. 双星形图方法高估约m^{3/4}倍
3. 本文的毛毛虫图方法高估约m^{3/5}倍
4. 所有方法的对数回归R-square > 0.98

Conclusion: 基于毛毛虫图的框架显著改进了多表连接大小上限估计精度，扩展了信息论方法在图同态统计中的应用，为数据库查询优化提供了更有效的工具。

Abstract: Recently, Abo Khamis et al. showed how to upper bound the size of a join of multiple tables, a problem essential to query optimization in database theory. They unified earlier works by the following information-theoretical framework.
  1. Let $(X_1,..., X_n)$ be a row selected from the join uniformly at random.
  2. The size of the join is now $\exp(H(X_1,..., X_n))$.
  3. To upper bound $H(X_1,..., X_n)$, break it into several $\textit{local entropies}$, such as $H(X_1)$, $H(X_2, X_3)$, and $H(X_4|X_5)$, using Shannon-type inequalities.
  4. Upper bound local entropies using statistics of the tables being joined.
  The statistics Abo Khamis et al. considered are the counts of graph homomorphisms from stars to the tables. In a follow-up work, we generalized stars to bi-stars. In this paper, we generalize bi-stars to caterpillars, an even larger class of graphs inspired by Sidorenko's conjecture. Simulations show that, while Abo Khamis et al.'s star bound overestimates the join size by $m$, our bi-star bound overestimates by about $m^{3/4}$, and this paper's new caterpillar bound overestimates by about $m^{3/5}$. These exponents are obtained by log-log regressions with R-square $> 0.98$. All homomorphisms are counted in time linear in the size of the tables being joined.

</details>


### [208] [Constructions of $q$-ary Golay Complementary Pairs Over Flexible Non-Power-of-Two Lengths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14667)
*Zhiye Yang,Keqin Feng*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 证明四元Golay互补对（q=4）的存在性等价于构造所有4h元GCPs（长度为2^mM），并通过扩展布尔函数实现灵活长度范围的直接构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Golay互补对自1951年提出后在通信系统中被广泛应用，但现有构造方法在长度灵活性上存在限制。本文旨在建立四元GCP存在性与更广泛GCP构造之间的等价关系，并提供更灵活的构造方法。

Method: 使用扩展布尔函数（EBFs）进行序列构造，证明四元GCP（q=4）长度为M的存在性等价于可显式构造所有4h元GCPs（长度为2^mM），其中h,m≥1为整数。

Result: 提出的直接构造方法能够产生比以往所有相关结果更灵活长度范围的GCPs。

Conclusion: 建立了四元GCP存在性与更广泛GCP构造之间的理论等价关系，并通过扩展布尔函数实现了长度范围更灵活的Golay互补对直接构造。

Abstract: Golay complementary pair (GCP), first introduced by Golay in 1951, has been extensively studied and widely applied in communication systems. A $q$-ary GCP $\{\mathbf{A},\mathbf{B}\}$ consists of two $q$-ary complex sequences $\mathbf{A}=(A_0,\cdots,A_{M-1})$ and $\mathbf{B}=({B}_0,\cdots,{B}_{M-1})$ of equal length $M$, where $\textit{A}_i,\textit{B}_i\in\{ξ^a:0\leq a\leq q-1\}$ with $ξ=e^{\frac{2π\sqrt{-1}}{q}}$.In this paper,we prove that the existence of a quaternary ($q=4$) GCP of length $M$ is equivalent to the explicit constructibility of ($4h$)-ary GCPs of length $2^mM$ for all integers $h,m\geq1$. All proposed sequences are constructed via extended Boolean functions (EBFs), and the direct construction yields GCPs with more flexible length ranges than all previous relevant results.

### [209] [Exploiting Correlations in Federated Learning: Opportunities and Practical Limitations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14751)
*Adrian Edin,Michel Kieffer,Mikael Johansson,Zheng Chen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出了一个基于相关性的联邦学习压缩技术分类框架，分析了结构、时间和空间三种相关性，并开发了自适应压缩设计


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习中通信瓶颈问题催生了大量的梯度压缩研究，现有方法基于不同类型的相关性假设，但缺乏系统性的分类和分析框架

Method: 1. 提出基于相关性类型（结构、时间、空间）的压缩技术分类框架；2. 分析这些相关性的来源并设计量化度量指标；3. 将现有压缩方法重新解释为该统一框架；4. 基于相关性强弱设计两种自适应压缩方案

Result: 实验表明：（1）结构、时间和空间相关性程度因任务复杂度、模型架构和算法配置而异；（2）自适应压缩方法相比传统非自适应方法在多种场景下都展现出明显性能优势

Abstract: The communication bottleneck in federated learning (FL) has spurred extensive research into techniques to reduce the volume of data exchanged between client devices and the central parameter server. In this paper, we systematically classify gradient and model compression schemes into three categories based on the type of correlations they exploit: structural, temporal, and spatial. We examine the sources of such correlations, propose quantitative metrics for measuring their magnitude, and reinterpret existing compression methods through this unified correlation-based framework. Our experimental studies demonstrate that the degrees of structural, temporal, and spatial correlations vary significantly depending on task complexity, model architecture, and algorithmic configurations. These findings suggest that algorithm designers should carefully evaluate correlation assumptions under specific deployment scenarios rather than assuming that they are always present. Motivated by these findings, we propose two adaptive compression designs that actively switch between different compression modes based on the measured correlation strength, and we evaluate their performance gains relative to conventional non-adaptive approaches. In summary, our unified taxonomy provides a clean and principled foundation for developing more effective and application-specific compression techniques for FL systems.

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在有限傅里叶曲线星座上使用切空间人工噪声的匹配与非匹配解码，分析了不同解码假设下高斯分布的符号相关协方差，推导了欧几里得成对误差的精确表达式，并给出了均匀星座的距离谱和符号误差界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在有限傅里叶曲线星座上，切空间人工噪声对匹配与非匹配解码性能的影响，旨在分析噪声比例和星座密度如何影响解码的不匹配行为。

Method: 使用有限傅里叶曲线星座，引入切空间人工噪声，对匹配解码采用高斯期望表示，对非匹配解码推导精确的欧几里得成对误差，并通过蒙特卡洛方法进行数值基准测试。

Result: 针对均匀偶数星座，欧几里得解码方面得到了显式的距离谱和符号误差界；匹配解码方面在反对称对上获得精确结果，并通过数值方法验证了全码本性能。

Conclusion: 通过分离切空间人工噪声在检测理论上的影响，这些结果从解析角度阐明了噪声比例和星座密度如何影响不匹配行为，但保密率的影响需要额外的信道和对手建模。

Abstract: We study matched and Euclidean-mismatched decoding on finite Fourier-curve constellations with tangent-space artificial noise. Each hypothesis induces a Gaussian law with symbol-dependent rank-one covariance. We derive exact Euclidean pairwise errors for arbitrary pairs and an exact Gaussian-expectation representation for matched decoding on bilaterally tangent-orthogonal pairs. For uniform even constellations, the Euclidean side yields explicit distance spectra and symbol-error bounds across all offset classes; the matched side is exact on antipodal pairs and benchmarked numerically at the full-codebook level via Monte Carlo. By isolating the detection-theoretic consequence of tangent-space artificial noise, these results clarify analytically how noise fraction and constellation density enter the mismatch behavior; secrecy-rate implications require additional channel and adversary modeling.

### [211] [Regret Tail Characterization of Optimal Bandit Algorithms with Generic Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14876)
*Subhodip Panda,Shubhada Agrawal*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该研究扩展了KLinf-UCB算法到非参数奖励分布类别，建立了其期望意义上的渐近最优性，并分析了遗憾尾部分布特性。针对有限支持的奖励分布情况，上界与已知下界精确匹配，为基于KL的渐近最优UCB算法提供了统一的严格遗憾尾部刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管在期望意义上渐近最优的算法可以最小化期望遗憾，但近期研究发现这类算法仍可能呈现重尾遗憾分布，即算法以不可忽略的概率产生大遗憾。现有对遗憾尾部的严格刻画多局限于参数模型（如单参数指数族），需要将分析扩展到更广泛的非参数分布类别。

Method: 将KLinf-UCB算法扩展到满足温和假设的广泛非参数奖励分布类别，建立算法在期望意义上的渐近最优性，然后分析其遗憾尾部行为，推导出遗憾尾部概率的新上界。

Result: 对于有限支持的奖励分布，所得上界与已知下界精确匹配；对于有界支撑和重尾（矩有界）老虎机模型，结果也能恢复相应的遗憾尾部保证。研究提供了基于KL的渐近最优UCB算法在非参数模型下的统一且严格的遗憾尾部刻画。

Conclusion: 该工作超越了传统的参数模型，为随机多臂老虎机中渐近最优算法的遗憾尾部行为提供了更全面的理论分析框架，将KLinf-UCB算法的尾部性能保证扩展到了广泛的非参数分布类别。

Abstract: We study the tail behavior of regret in stochastic multi-armed bandits for algorithms that are asymptotically optimal in expectation. While minimizing expected regret is the classical objective, recent work shows that even such algorithms can exhibit heavy regret tails, incurring large regret with non-negligible probability. Existing sharp characterizations of regret tails are largely restricted to parametric settings, such as single-parameter exponential families.
  In this work, we extend the $\KLinf$-UCB algorithm of to a broad nonparametric class of reward distributions satisfying mild assumptions, and establish its asymptotic optimality in expectation. We then analyze the tail behavior of its regret and derive a novel upper bound on the regret tail probability. As special cases, our results recover regret-tail guarantees for both bounded-support and heavy-tailed (moment-bounded) bandit models. Moreover, for the special case of finitely-supported reward distributions, our upper bound matches the known lower bound exactly. Our results thus provide a unified and tight characterization of regret tails for asymptotically optimal KL-based UCB algorithms, going beyond parametric models.

### [212] [Support Size of $\varepsilon$-Capacity-Achieving Inputs for the Amplitude-Constrained AWGN Channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14915)
*Luca Barletta,Alex Dytso*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 研究了幅度约束AWGN信道中，为实现容量接近ε的离散输入所需的最小支撑点数K_ε(A)的渐进缩放行为，揭示了ε在不同衰减速率下对应的不同缩放规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 幅度约束AWGN信道容量最优输入是离散的，但确切支撑点数量随幅度约束缩放的规律尚未解决。为绕过这一困难，转而研究实现容量ε近似的离散输入所需的最小支撑点数，这一放松形式化更易于分析且能揭示数值研究中观察到的不同缩放规律的本质原因。

Method: 采用近似理论中高斯混合的逼近界限与信息论中通过χ^2散度控制熵的技术，结合将问题关联到圆周上均匀分布逼近的环绕论证方法，分析K_ε(A)在不同ε衰减机制下的渐进行为。

Result: 当ε多项式衰减（ε=A^{-β}, β≥1）时，K_ε(A)=Θ(A√log A)；当ε指数小时，K_ε(A)的界在A√log A到A^{3/2}之间。证明了不同缩放规律对应ε最优性的不同机制，而非精确最优解的内在特性。

Conclusion: 通过研究容量ε近似所需最小离散输入支撑点数，提供了幅度约束AWGN信道离散输入渐进行为的系统化理论框架，解释了先前数值研究中观察到的多样性缩放规律，为相关编码设计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the amplitude-constrained additive white Gaussian noise (AWGN) channel from the perspective of near-optimal input distributions. While it is known that the capacity-achieving input is discrete with finitely many mass points, the precise scaling of its support size as a function of the amplitude constraint remains an open problem. In this work, we instead consider the minimal support size required to achieve capacity up to an $\varepsilon$-gap. We introduce the quantity $K_\varepsilon(A)$, defined as the smallest support size among discrete inputs supported on $[-A,A]$ that achieves mutual information within $\varepsilon$ of capacity. We show that this relaxed formulation is significantly more tractable and admits sharp characterizations across different regimes of $\varepsilon$. In particular, when $\varepsilon$ decays polynomially with $A$, i.e., $\varepsilon = A^{-β}$ for $β\geq 1$, we establish that $K_\varepsilon(A) = Θ(A\sqrt{\log A})$. For exponentially small gaps, we obtain bounds of order between $A\sqrt{\log A}$ and $A^{3/2}$. Our approach combines approximation-theoretic bounds for Gaussian mixtures with information-theoretic control of entropy via $χ^2$-divergence, together with a wrapping argument that relates the problem to approximating the uniform distribution on the circle. Beyond the technical results, our framework provides a conceptual explanation for the variety of scaling laws observed in prior numerical studies, showing that these correspond to different regimes of $\varepsilon$-optimality rather than intrinsic properties of the exact optimizer.

</details>


### [213] [Explicit Constant-Alphabet Subspace Design Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15218)
*Rohan Goyal,Venkatesan Guruswami,Jun-Ting Hsieh*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 构建了明确的第一类恒定字母大小的子空间设计码（subspace design codes），回答了之前的工作中提出的开放性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 之前的工作证明了子空间设计码在局部性质上具有类似于随机线性码的性能，但已知的显式构造（如折叠Reed-Solomon码和重数码）需要字母表大小随码长多项式增长。构建显式的恒定字母子空间设计码是一个开放问题。

Method: 使用基于扩展图的Alon-Edmonds-Luby（AEL）框架构建子空间设计码，该框架被推广用于获得恒定字母大小。

Result: 成功构造了显式的恒定字母子空间设计码，并在参数上带来了一些改进，特别是在列表恢复（list-recovery）方面。

Conclusion: 本工作使用AEL框架解决了恒定字母子空间设计码的构造问题，为子空间设计码的局部性质与随机线性码的相似性提供了统一的理论基础，并在列表恢复方面取得了参数上的改进。

Abstract: The subspace design property for additive codes is a higher-dimensional generalization of the minimum distance property. As shown recently by Brakensiek, Chen, Dhar and Zhang, it implies that the code has similar performance as random linear codes with respect to all "local properties". Explicit algebraic codes, such as folded Reed-Solomon and multiplicity codes, are known to have the subspace design property, but they need alphabet sizes that grow as a large polynomial in the block length. Constructing explicit constant-alphabet subspace design codes was subsequently posed as an open question in Brakensiek, Chen, Dhar and Zhang.
  In this work, we answer their question and give explicit constructions of subspace design codes over constant-sized alphabets, using the expander-based Alon-Edmonds-Luby (AEL) framework. This generalizes the recent work of Jeronimo and Shagrithaya, which showed that such codes share local properties of random linear codes. Our work obtains this consequence in a unified manner via the subspace design property. In addition, our approach yields some improvements in parameters for list-recovery.

</details>


### [214] [Bandwidth Cost of Locally Repairable Convertible Codes in the Global Merge Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15282)
*Saransh Chopra,Shubhransh Singhvi,K. V. Rashmi*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究分布式存储系统中可转换码在本地可修复码背景下的带宽成本，针对全局合并场景推导出首个非平凡下界，证明现有构建方案在特定参数范围内是带宽最优的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式存储系统通过根据磁盘故障率调整冗余级别可以显著节省空间，但现有的代码转换过程通常资源密集。可转换码旨在高效实现这种转换同时保持理想的解码性约束，如修复度。本文重点关注转换过程中数据传输的带宽成本问题。

Method: 研究工作集中在系统最优距离本地可修复码之间的转换带宽成本，特别关注全局合并机制——多个初始码字合并为单个最终码字同时保持信息局部性。采用稳定的可转换码方法（最大化转换过程中未改变节点数量），将信息论方法推广到LRC设置，推导出带宽成本的非平凡下界，且不依赖任何线性假设。

Result: 推导出全局合并机制下转换带宽成本的第一个非平凡下界，证明Maturana和Rashmi的构造在广泛参数范围内是带宽最优的。这些下界具有普遍性，适用于线性和非线性编码方案。

Conclusion: 本文建立了本地可修复码转换带宽成本的理论界限，为分布式存储系统的代码转换效率提供了理论基础，并验证了现有构造在重要参数范围内的最优性，对实际系统设计具有指导意义。

Abstract: Recent studies have shown that distributed storage systems can achieve significant space savings by adapting redundancy levels to varying disk failure rates. This adaptation is performed via code conversion, wherein data encoded under an initial code are transformed to data encoded under a final code. While this process is typically resource-intensive, convertible codes are designed to enable these transformations efficiently while preserving desirable decodability constraints such as repair degree, or the number of nodes accessed during node repair.
  In this work, we focus on the bandwidth cost of conversion, or the total amount of data transferred during the conversion process. We study fundamental limits on the bandwidth cost of conversion between systematic optimal-distance Locally Repairable Codes (LRCs). We restrict our focus to the global merge regime, in which multiple initial codewords are combined to form a single final codeword while preserving information locality. We focus on stable convertible codes, wherein the number of unchanged nodes is maximized during conversion. We generalize an information-theoretic approach for modeling code conversion to the LRC setting, and derive the first non-trivial lower bounds on the bandwidth cost of conversion in this regime. Notably, our bounds do not rely on any linearity assumptions. Consequently, we show that the constructions of Maturana and Rashmi are bandwidth-optimal across a broad range of parameters in the global merge regime.

</details>


### [215] [Reed--Muller Codes Achieve the Symmetric Capacity on Finite-State Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.15295)
*Henry D. Pfister,Navin Kashyap,Jean-Francois Chamberland,Galen Reeves*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究在有限状态信道中使用RM码实现可靠通信，证明了经随机扰乱的二进制RM码序列可达到二元输入不可分解有限状态信道的对称容量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于扩展近期针对无记忆信道的对称性分析方法到有限状态信道，探索利用RM码实现信道容量的途径。

Method: 方法包括三个部分：建立双向传递群码在离散无记忆信道上的容量对称定理；通过分组和交织将二元输入有限状态信道转化为近似无记忆的非二元信道；证明交织后的非二元码可由单个二进制RM码构建。

Result: 研究结果表明，经过随机扰乱的二进制RM码序列能够达到二元输入不可分解有限状态信道的对称容量（或均匀输入信息率）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将对称性分析方法扩展到有限状态信道，为RM码在这类信道中的应用提供了理论基础，展示了二进制RM码在实现信道容量方面的潜力。

Abstract: We study reliable communication over finite-state channels (FSCs) using Reed--Muller (RM) codes. Building on recent symmetry-based analyses for memoryless channels, we show that a sequence of binary RM codes (with some random scrambling) can achieve the symmetric capacity (or uniform-input information rate) of a binary-input indecomposable FSC.
  Our approach has three components. First, we establish a capacity-via-symmetry theorem for doubly-transitive group codes on discrete memoryless channels (DMCs) with non-binary inputs, under some symmetry and puncturing conditions. Then, we reduce a binary-input FSC to an almost memoryless non-binary channel by grouping adjacent input bits into blocks and interleaving non-binary codes onto the channel. Finally, we show that the interleaved non-binary codes can be constructed from a single binary RM code.

</details>
